######JEs & HISTORICAL#######

#Panum 11: The Germ Theory
panum.11 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.11.t

	desc = panum.11.d

	flavor = panum.11.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_germ_theory.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#
		name = panum.11.g
		panum_add_germ_theory_effect = yes
	}
}

#Panum 12: The First Vaccine
panum.12 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.12.t

	desc = panum.12.d

	flavor = panum.12.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		game_date < 1836.1.1
		has_technology_researched = panum_vaccination_tech
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = theiler_smallpox_vaccine_invented_global_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = theiler_smallpox_vaccine_invented_global_var
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit ={
				NOT = {
					has_variable = panum_physician_var
				}
			}
			create_new_character_base_effect = { CHARACTER = physician PROJECT = panum }
			panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#
		name = panum.12.g
		theiler_add_smallpox_vaccine_effect = yes
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 50 }
		panum_medium_add_technology = yes
	}
}

######FREE PHYSICIANS######

#Panum 21: Triage
panum.21 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.21.t

	desc = panum.21.d

	flavor = panum.21.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = triage
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_triage_invented_global_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_triage_invented_global_var
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = panum_physician_var
				}
			}
			create_new_character_base_effect = { CHARACTER = physician PROJECT = panum }
			panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#
		name = panum.21.g
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 60 }
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					scope:panum_physician_scope = {
						has_trait = panum_surgeon
					}
				}
			}
			scope:panum_physician_scope = {
				add_trait = panum_surgeon
			}
		}
	}
}

		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_psychiatry_invented_global_var
		}
	}

		set_global_variable = panum_psychiatry_invented_global_var
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		if = {

					has_variable = panum_physician_var
				}
			}

		name = panum.23.g
		panum_add_x_psycho_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 60 }

			limit = {

					}
				}
			}

######PHYSICIAN ACTIONS######

#Panum 51: Describe Local Disease
panum.51 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.51.t

	desc = panum.51.d

	flavor = panum.51.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cancellation_trigger = {
		panum_has_epidemic_trigger = no
	}

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Cholera
		name = panum.51.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_journal_entry = je_panum_cholera
			panum_has_cholera_description_trigger = no
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_panum_cholera_description
		}
	}

	option = {	#Tuberculosis
		name = panum.51.h
		trigger = {
			has_journal_entry = je_panum_tuberculosis
			panum_has_tuberculosis_description_trigger = no

#Panum 54: Treat Foreign Disease
panum.54 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.54.t

	desc = panum.54.d

	flavor = panum.52.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cancellation_trigger = {
		panum_can_find_foreign_treatment_trigger = no
	}

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#Can root country find treatment?
				panum_has_cholera_description_trigger = yes
				panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = no
				panum_cholera_research_tech_requirement_trigger = yes
				#Is there a country with the disease?
				any_country = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_cholera
					NOT = {
						ROOT = this
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_cholera
					NOT = {
						ROOT = this
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = panum_cholera_country_scope
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#Can root country find treatment?
				panum_has_tuberculosis_description_trigger = yes
				panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
				panum_tuberculosis_research_tech_requirement_trigger = yes
				#Is there a country with the disease?
				any_country = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_tuberculosis
					NOT = {
						ROOT = this
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_tuberculosis
					NOT = {
						ROOT = this
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = panum_tuberculosis_country_scope
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#Can root country find treatment?
				panum_has_smallpox_description_trigger = yes
				panum_has_smallpox_treatment_trigger = no
				panum_smallpox_research_tech_requirement_trigger = yes
				#Is there a country with the disease?
				any_country = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_smallpox
					NOT = {
						ROOT = this
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_smallpox
					NOT = {
						ROOT = this
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = panum_smallpox_country_scope
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				#Can root country find treatment?
				panum_has_typhus_description_trigger = yes
				panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = no
				panum_typhus_research_tech_requirement_trigger = yes
				#Is there a country with the disease?
				any_country = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_typhus
					NOT = {
						ROOT = this
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_diplomatic_relevance = ROOT
					has_journal_entry = je_panum_typhus

					}

			}

#Panum 55: Event informing the player that foreign disease description is possible
panum.55 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.55.t

	desc = panum.55.d

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_cholera.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	cancellation_trigger = {
		panum_has_active_physician_no_tooltip_trigger = no
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {	#Send our Physician immediately!
		name = panum.55.g
		default_option = yes

		set_variable = panum_physician_action_active_var
		set_variable = panum_physician_describe_disease_foreign_active_var
		trigger_event = { 
			id = panum.52
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Not right now.
		name = panum.55.h
		default_option = yes
	}

	option = {	#Only fire notifications
		name = panum.55.i
		default_option = yes

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_foreign_disease_research_only_notification_tt
			set_variable = panum_foreign_disease_research_only_notification_var
		}
	}

	option = {	#No more reminders
		name = panum.55.j
		default_option = yes

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_foreign_disease_research_no_notification_tt
			set_variable = panum_foreign_disease_research_no_notification_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 61: Treatment Team finishes work
panum.61 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.61.t

	desc = panum.61.d

	flavor = panum.61.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		video = "unspecific_sick_in_hospital"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_overlord_or_above = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
                    is_direct_subject_of = prev
                }
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_overlord_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Our overlord takes care of us?
		name = panum.61.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_cholera_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_tuberculosis_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_smallpox_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_smallpox_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_smallpox_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_typhus_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_yellow_fever_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_yellow_fever_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_yellow_fever_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_measles_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_measles_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_measles_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_scarlet_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_scarlet_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_scarlet_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_plague_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_plague_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_plague_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_diphteria_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_diphteria_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_diphteria_treatment_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
					panum_has_polio_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				panum_has_polio_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_polio_treatment_effect = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
				post_notification = panum_overlord_medical_treatment_team_notification
			}
		}
	}
}

			theiler_add_polio_vaccine_effect = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:panum_overlord_scope = {
				post_notification = panum_overlord_medical_vaccination_team_notification
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_cholera_state_effect = yes
	}

		name = panum.100.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}

					type = je_panum_cholera
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_cholera_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	desc = panum.101.d

	flavor = panum.100.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_cholera.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_third_cholera_global_var
		}
		game_date >= 1846.1.1 #We start with the third wave
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_EAST_BENGAL
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_third_cholera_global_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_EAST_BENGAL
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_panum_cholera
		}
	}

	option = {	#Somehow, Cholera returned
		name = panum.101.g
		default_option = yes
		s:STATE_EAST_BENGAL = {
			start_harvest_condition = panum_cholera_condition
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_player = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_player = yes
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = panum.102
						days = { 20 30 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 103: Cholera in Factory
panum.103 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.103.t

	desc = panum.103.d

	flavor = panum.103.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_cholera.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 3
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_cholera_trigger = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_group = bg_manufacturing
			}
			NOT = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_group = bg_manufacturing
					has_modifier = panum_factory_quarantine_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_cholera_trigger = yes
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_group = bg_manufacturing
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_group = bg_manufacturing
						has_modifier = panum_factory_quarantine_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Quarantine the Factories!
		name = panum.103.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			every_scope_building = {
				limit = {
					is_building_group = bg_manufacturing
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_factory_quarantine_modifier
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#The factories must continue to run, at all costs!
		name = panum.103.h
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = laborers
				percent = 0.005
			}
		}
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = machinists
				percent = 0.003
			}
		}
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = engineers
				percent = 0.001
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 104: CHARACTER gets Cholera!
panum.104 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.104.t

	desc = panum.104.d

	flavor = panum.104.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 3
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_character = {
			NOR = {
				has_trait = panum_cholera
				has_variable = panum_cholera_immunity_var
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_trait = panum_cholera
					has_variable = panum_cholera_immunity_var
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = disease_victim_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Ensures the best possible treatment!
		name = panum.104.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_personal_treatment_cost_modifier
		}
		scope:disease_victim_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_cholera
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_personal_treatment_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Call Doctor Hasenbein!
		name = panum.104.h
		trigger = {
			has_variable = panum_physician_var
		}
		scope:disease_victim_scope = {
			set_variable = panum_cholera_immunity_var
		}
	}

	option = {	#He's not that important...
		name = panum.104.i
		scope:disease_victim_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_cholera
		}
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = { 
				scope:disease_victim_scope = {
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

				percent = 0.003
			}
		}
	}

		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_x_cholera_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}

		panum_remove_new_physician_effect = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.120.t

	desc = panum.120.d

	flavor = panum.120.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_cholera.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {	#But at what cost?
		name = panum.120.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = panum_cholera_treatment_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = panum_cholera_treatment_modifier
		}
	}

}

#Panum 132: News from the Medical Observation Expedition (hidden)
panum.132 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		panum_add_description_expedition_clue_effect = yes
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
			}
			add = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_physician_famous
			}
			add = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_physician_experienced
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = dubois_naturalist
					has_trait = dubois_naturalist_experienced
					has_trait = dubois_naturalist_famous
				}
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

#Panum 138: Disease Description (Expedition)
panum.138 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.138.t

	desc = panum.138.d

	flavor = panum.138.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the description title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_description_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_description_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#DISEASE is losing its horror.
		name = panum.138.g
		panum_add_disease_description_effect = yes
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_description_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 140: Cholera Treatment
panum.140 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.140.t

	desc = panum.140.d

	flavor = panum.140.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_cholera_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Cholera is losing its horror.
		name = panum.140.g
		panum_add_cholera_treatment_effect = yes
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 8 }
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 141: The Brewery
panum.141 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.141.t

	desc = panum.141.d

	flavor = panum.141.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_1.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.141.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_cholera_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

#Panum 142: Creatures of Habit
panum.142 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.142.t

	desc = panum.142.d

	flavor = panum.142.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_2.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_cholera_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.142.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_cholera_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			has_trait = reckless
		}
		NOT = {
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				has_trait = panum_cholera
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_cholera_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.162.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_cholera_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 4 }
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			add_trait = panum_cholera
		}
		random_list = {
			65 = {}
			35 = { 
				var:panum_physician_var = {
					kill_physician_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Dissuade the doctor from this foolhardy maneuver!
		name = panum.162.h
		panum_add_x_cholera_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = -1 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 200: Tuberculosis epidemic
panum.200 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.200.t

	desc = panum.200.d

	flavor = panum.200.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_tuberculosis.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_tuberculosis_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Tuberculosis!
		name = panum.200.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_tuberculosis
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_tuberculosis_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Panum 202: A hereditary disease?
panum.202 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.202.t

	desc = panum.202.d

	flavor = panum.202.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_tuberculosis.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_tuberculosis_contagious_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#It is a hereditary disease and there is nothing we can do.
		name = panum.202.g
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			1 = {}
			1 = {
				scope:panum_disease_state = {
					kill_population_percent_in_state = {
						percent = 0.002
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#It is a contagious disease and we must do everything we can to stop it from spreading!
		name = panum.202.h
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_tuberculosis_contagious_var
			years = 3
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_tuberculosis_quarantine_modifier
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.01
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 203: Spitting on the streets
panum.203 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.203.t

	desc = panum.203.d

	flavor = panum.203.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_tuberculosis.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 24
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = panum_forbidden_spitting_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = panum_forbidden_spitting_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Ban this disgusting habit!
		name = panum.203.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_forbidden_spitting_modifier
				days = 100
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.01
				strata = lower
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Announce a draconian ban and make the evildoers pay!
		name = panum.203.h
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = 100000
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_forbidden_spitting_modifier
				days = 365
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.02
				strata = lower
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Spitting is a human nature that cannot be banned.
		name = panum.203.i
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				strata = lower
				percent = 0.003
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 204: ARTIST gets Tuberculosis
panum.204 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.204.t

	desc = panum.204.d

	flavor = panum.204.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:disease_victim_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 3
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_variable = elgar_composer_var
				var:elgar_composer_var ?= {
					NOR = {
						has_trait = panum_tuberculosis
						has_variable = panum_tuberculosis_immunity_var
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = manzoni_writer_var
				var:manzoni_writer_var ?= {
					NOR = {
						has_trait = panum_tuberculosis
						has_variable = panum_tuberculosis_immunity_var
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_variable = klimt_painter_var
				var:klimt_painter_var ?= {
					NOR = {
						has_trait = panum_tuberculosis
						has_variable = panum_tuberculosis_immunity_var
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = elgar_composer_var
				var:elgar_composer_var ?= {
					NOR = {
						has_trait = panum_tuberculosis
						has_variable = panum_tuberculosis_immunity_var
					}
				}
			}
			var:elgar_composer_var ?= {
				save_scope_as = disease_victim_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = manzoni_writer_var
				var:manzoni_writer_var ?= {
					NOR = {
						has_trait = panum_tuberculosis
						has_variable = panum_tuberculosis_immunity_var
					}
				}
			}
			var:manzoni_writer_var ?= {
				save_scope_as = disease_victim_scope
			}
		}
		else = {
			var:klimt_painter_var ?= {
				save_scope_as = disease_victim_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Ensures the best possible treatment!
		name = panum.104.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_personal_treatment_cost_modifier
		}
		scope:disease_victim_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_tuberculosis
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_personal_treatment_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Call Doctor Hasenbein!
		name = panum.104.h
		trigger = {
			has_variable = panum_physician_var
		}
		scope:disease_victim_scope = {
			set_variable = panum_tuberculosis_immunity_var
		}
	}

	option = {	#Wouldn't that be an inspiring occasion for a requiem?
		name = panum.204.i
		trigger = {
			scope:disease_victim_scope = {
				has_variable = mr_is_composer_var
			}
		}
		scope:disease_victim_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_tuberculosis
		}
		elgar_add_x_music_tradition_unscaled_effect = { AMOUNT = 20 }
		composer_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = { 
				kill_composer_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#But hasn't tuberculosis always been the subject of writers?
		name = panum.204.j
		trigger = {
			scope:disease_victim_scope = {
				has_variable = mr_is_writer_var
			}
		}
		scope:disease_victim_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_tuberculosis
		}
		manzoni_add_x_literary_tradition_unscaled_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		writer_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {

			}
		}

#Panum 205: Tuberculosis Sanatorium
panum.205 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.205.t

	desc = panum.205.d

	flavor = panum.205.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_tuberculosis.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			any_scope_state = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_panum_tuberculosis_sanatorium
				}
			}
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:north_german
				any_scope_state = {
					state_region = s:STATE_LOWER_SILESIA #Görbersdorf
					is_incorporated = yes
				}
			}
			any_scope_state = {
				is_incorporated = yes
				OR = {
					douglas_state_has_mountain_range_trigger = yes
					douglas_state_has_mountain_summit_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				c:SWI ?= this
				any_scope_state = {
					state_region = s:STATE_EAST_SWITZERLAND #Davos
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					state_region = s:STATE_EAST_SWITZERLAND #Davos
				}
				save_scope_as = panum_davos_scope
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_has_primary_culture = cu:north_german
				any_scope_state = {
					state_region = s:STATE_LOWER_SILESIA #Görbersdorf
					is_incorporated = yes
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					state_region = s:STATE_LOWER_SILESIA
				}
				save_scope_as = panum_davos_scope
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_incorporated = yes
					OR = {
						douglas_state_has_mountain_range_trigger = yes
						douglas_state_has_mountain_summit_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = panum_davos_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Build a Sanatorium in STATE!
		name = panum.205.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			add_treasury = -100000
		}
		scope:panum_davos_scope = {
			set_variable = panum_sanatorium_possible_var
			start_building_construction = building_panum_tuberculosis_sanatorium
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
	}

	option = {	#This is all just luxurious charlatanry.
		name = panum.205.h

		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					c:SWI ?= this
				}
				add = -20
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 206: The disease of the proletarians
panum.206 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.206.t

	desc = panum.206.d

	flavor = panum.206.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:union_leader

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = panum_help_against_tuberculosis_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = panum_help_against_tuberculosis_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			save_scope_as = trade_unions_ig 
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = union_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Maybe the poor should just wash themselves more?
		name = panum.206.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = manzoni_political_tailwind_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.01
				strata = lower
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Selective improvements in this area are warranted.
		name = panum.206.h
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_help_against_tuberculosis_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#The question of health care is a national matter.
		name = panum.206.i
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_public_health_insurance
					value > neutral
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_supports_health_care_initiative_modifier
				years = 3
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = manzoni_political_tailwind_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		every_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				law_stance = {
					law = law_type:law_public_health_insurance
					value < neutral
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_opposes_health_care_initiative_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Applause for this initiative!
		name = panum.206.j
		trigger = {
			scope:trade_unions_ig = {
				is_in_government = yes
			}
		}
		scope:trade_unions_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_praised_for_tuberculosis_initiative_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 207: Religious Initiative
panum.207 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.207.t

	desc = panum.207.d

	flavor = panum.207.f
	
	duration = 3

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = panum_tuberculosis_hospital_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = panum_tuberculosis_hospital_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		ig:ig_devout = {
			save_scope_as = devout_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = devout_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#These storytellers are just trying to gain influence!
		name = panum.207.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				percent = 0.001
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Applause for this initiative!
		name = panum.206.j
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_tuberculosis_hospital_modifier
			}
		}
		scope:devout_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_praised_for_tuberculosis_initiative_modifier
				years = 3
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = manzoni_political_tailwind_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

}

	cooldown = {
		months = 12
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_physician = no
		any_scope_state = {
			has_building = building_panum_tuberculosis_sanatorium
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		create_new_character_base_effect = { CHARACTER = physician PROJECT = panum }
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_tuberculosis_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Give him an official position immediately!
		name = panum.112.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100 #AI will always take the Physician
		}
	}

	option = {	#The doctor should train future generations to fight the next epidemic.
		name = panum.112.h
		panum_medium_add_technology = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				panum_has_tuberculosis_treatment_trigger = no
			}
			panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}

		panum_remove_new_physician_effect = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Panum 240: Tuberculosis Treatment
panum.240 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.240.t

	desc = panum.240.d

	flavor = panum.240.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Tuberculosis is losing its horror.
		name = panum.140.g
		panum_add_tuberculosis_treatment_effect = yes
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 8 }
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:panum_physician_var ?= {
					has_trait = panum_tuberculosis
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				remove_trait = panum_tuberculosis
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_disease_state = {
					has_modifier = panum_epidemic_tuberculosis_severe_modifier
				}
			}
			scope:panum_disease_state = {
				remove_modifier = panum_epidemic_tuberculosis_severe_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_disease_state = {
					has_modifier = panum_epidemic_tuberculosis_normal_modifier
				}
			}
			scope:panum_disease_state = {
				remove_modifier = panum_epidemic_tuberculosis_normal_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:panum_disease_state = {
					has_modifier = panum_epidemic_tuberculosis_mild_modifier
				}
			}
			scope:panum_disease_state = {
				remove_modifier = panum_epidemic_tuberculosis_mild_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 241: The Rabbit Experiment
panum.241 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.241.t

	desc = panum.241.d

	flavor = panum.241.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_1.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
		NOT = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = charismatic
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
	}

	option = {	#Stop these terrible animal experiments!
		name = panum.241.g
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				var:panum_physician_var = {
					has_trait = cruel
				}
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			add_trait = charismatic
		}
	}

	option = {	#Let's repeat the experiment to be sure.
		name = panum.241.h
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						has_trait = cruel
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {}
				1 = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						add_trait = cruel
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#A third rabbit experiment for science!
		name = panum.241.i
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		set_variable = panum_cruel_tuberculosis_experiments_var
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						has_trait = cruel
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {}
				2 = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						add_trait = cruel
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#The Doctor may kill as many rabbits as possible to proof his theory.
		name = panum.241.j
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 4 }
		theiler_add_x_tuberculosis_pathogen_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		set_variable = panum_cruel_tuberculosis_experiments_var
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						has_trait = cruel
					}
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				add_trait = cruel
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = cruel
			}
			add = 4
		}
	}
}

#Panum 261: Artificial Pneumothorax
panum.261 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.261.t

	desc = panum.261.d

	flavor = panum.261.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_1.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
			has_variable = panum_pneumothorax_var
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			OR = {
				has_trait = engineer
				has_trait = innovative
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		set_variable = panum_pneumothorax_var
	}

	option = {	#It's about saving human lives.
		name = panum.263.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = panum_pneumothorax_global_var
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = panum_pneumothorax_global_var
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				set_variable = {
					name = panum_physician_achievement_pneumothorax_inventor_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_pneumothorax_inventor_loc
				}
			}
			panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_pneumothorax_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 262: Thoracoplasty
panum.262 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.262.t

	desc = panum.262.d

	flavor = panum.262.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_2.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
			has_variable = panum_thoracoplasty_var
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			has_trait = panum_surgeon
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		set_variable = panum_thoracoplasty_var
	}

	option = {	#It's about saving human lives.
		name = panum.263.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = panum_thoracoplasty_global_var
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = panum_thoracoplasty_global_var
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				set_variable = {
					name = panum_physician_achievement_thoracoplasty_inventor_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_thoracoplasty_inventor_loc
				}
			}
			panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_thoracoplasty_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 263: The Doctor did it again!
panum.263 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.263.t

	desc = panum.263.d

	flavor = panum.263.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_3.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
		has_variable = panum_cruel_tuberculosis_experiments_var
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
	}

	option = {	#It's about saving human lives.
		name = panum.263.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						has_trait = psychological_affliction
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				9 = {}
				1 = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						add_trait = psychological_affliction
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#This doctor has a serious problem.
		name = panum.263.h
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

#Panum 264: De Contagione
panum.264 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.264.t

	desc = panum.264.d

	flavor = panum.264.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_4.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 50 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
			has_variable = panum_fracastoro_var
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			OR = {
				has_trait = erudite
				has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist
				has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_experienced
				has_trait = lepsius_archaeologist_famous
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		set_variable = panum_fracastoro_var
	}

	option = {	#This will spur the search for treatment.
		name = panum.264.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#This is much more convincing than the miasma theory.
		name = panum.264.h
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
	}

	option = {	#Could a small pathogen cause tuberculosis?
		name = panum.264.i
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_tuberculosis_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		theiler_add_x_tuberculosis_pathogen_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 300: Smallpox epidemic
panum.300 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.300.t

	desc = panum.300.d

	flavor = panum.300.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_smallpox.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_smallpox_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Smallpox!
		name = panum.300.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_smallpox
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_smallpox_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_smallpox_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Panum 303: Smallpox out of control
panum.303 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.303.t

	desc = panum.303.d

	flavor = panum.303.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_smallpox.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 6
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_smallpox_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_smallpox_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_smallpox_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Is there no cure for this terrible illness?
		name = panum.303.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				percent = 0.002
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 340: Smallpox Treatment
panum.340 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.340.t

	desc = panum.340.d

	flavor = panum.340.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Smallpox is losing its horror.
		name = panum.340.g
		panum_add_smallpox_treatment_effect = yes
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 400: Typhus epidemic
panum.400 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.400.t

	desc = panum.400.d

	flavor = panum.400.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_typhus.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_typhus_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Typhus!
		name = panum.400.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_typhus
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_typhus_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Panum 402: A disease of moral corruption?
panum.402 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.402.t

	desc = panum.402.d

	flavor = panum.402.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_typhus.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#There is a reason why typhus primarily affects criminals, prostitutes and immoral soldiers.
		name = panum.402.g
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			1 = {}
			1 = {
				scope:panum_disease_state = {
					kill_population_percent_in_state = {
						percent = 0.001
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#It probably matters less what these people are than where they live.
		name = panum.402.h
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata =upper
				value = 0.05
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = middle
				value = 0.03
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				strata = lower
				value = 0.01
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 403: Quarantine

	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#The whole area should be quarantined.
		name = panum.403.g
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata =upper
				value = 0.03
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = middle
				value = 0.02
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_typhus_quarantine_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Take the typhus sufferers to special houses.
		name = panum.403.h
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				strata =upper
				value = 0.03
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				strata = middle
				value = 0.02
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = lower
				value = 0.01
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_typhus_fever_sheds_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Typhus is not a contagious disease, so quarantine makes no sense.
		name = panum.403.i
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				strata = lower
				percent = 0.005
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 404: Filthy Sheds
panum.404 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.404.t

	desc = panum.404.d

	flavor = panum.404.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_typhus.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 3
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
			has_modifier = panum_typhus_fever_sheds_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
				has_modifier = panum_typhus_fever_sheds_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#We can't risk more people becoming infected.
		name = panum.404.g
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_typhus_rigid_rules_modifier
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = lower
				value = 0.01
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Improve the situation of typhus sufferers and provide medical help.
		name = panum.404.h
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_typhus_fever_sheds_help_modifier
		}
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				strata = lower
				value = 0.01
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {}
				1 = {
					scope:panum_disease_state = {
						kill_population_percent_in_state = {
							percent = 0.001
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Dismantle these inhumane houses!
		name = panum.404.i
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			remove_modifier = panum_typhus_fever_sheds_modifier
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				percent = 0.002
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata =upper
				value = 0.02
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = middle
				value = 0.02
			}
			add_loyalists_in_state = {
				strata = lower
				value = 0.02
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 407: Typhus in Barracks
panum.407 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.407.t

	desc = panum.407.d

	flavor = panum.407.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_typhus.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 2
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_typhus_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
			has_building = building_barrack
			NOT = {
				any_scope_building = {
					has_modifier = panum_typhus_barracks_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
				has_building = building_barrack
				NOT = {
					any_scope_building = {
						has_modifier = panum_typhus_barracks_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#No! They were destined for an honorable death on the battlefield!
		name = panum.407.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			every_scope_building = {
				limit = {
					is_building_group = bg_army
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_typhus_barracks_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = soldiers
				percent = 0.003
			}
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = officers
				percent = 0.001
			}
		}
	}

}

				has_trait = meticulous
			}
			add = 1
		}

#Panum 440: Typhus Treatment
panum.440 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.440.t

	desc = panum.440.d

	flavor = panum.440.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_typhus_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Typhus is losing its horror.
		name = panum.440.g
		panum_add_typhus_treatment_effect = yes
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 4 }
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:panum_physician_var ?= {
					has_trait = panum_typhus
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				remove_trait = panum_typhus
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.441.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_typhus_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 454: Sick
panum.454 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.454.t

	desc = panum.454.d

	flavor = panum.454.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_investigation_4.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
		NOT = {
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				has_trait = panum_typhus
			}
		}	
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.454.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_typhus_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = -1 }
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.454.h
		default_option = yes
		random_list = {
			55 = {}
			35 = {
				var:panum_physician_var = {
					add_trait = panum_typhus
				}
			}
			10 = {
				var:panum_physician_var = {
					kill_physician_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 500: Yellow Fever epidemic
panum.500 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.500.t

	desc = panum.500.d

	flavor = panum.500.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_yellow_fever.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_yellow_fever_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Yellow Fever
		name = panum.500.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_yellow_fever
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_yellow_fever_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_yellow_fever_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Panum 502: A contagious disease?
panum.502 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.502.t

	desc = panum.502.d

	flavor = panum.502.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_yellow_fever.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_yellow_fever_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#It is a contagious disease and we must do everything we can to stop it from spreading!
		name = panum.202.h
		default_option = yes
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_yellow_fever_quarantine_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#There is no evidence that this is a contagious disease.
		name = panum.502.g
		default_option = yes
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata =upper
				value = 0.03
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = middle
				value = 0.02
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 503: Yellow Fever affects Plantations
panum.503 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.503.t

	desc = panum.503.d

	flavor = panum.503.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_yellow_fever.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_yellow_fever_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_group = bg_plantations
			}
			NOT = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_group = bg_plantations
					has_modifier = panum_plantation_quarantine_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_group = bg_plantations
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_group = bg_plantations
						has_modifier = panum_plantation_quarantine_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Get the workers out of the fields!
		name = panum.503.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			every_scope_building = {
				limit = {
					is_building_group = bg_plantations
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_plantation_quarantine_modifier
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#The plantation must continue to run, at all costs!
		name = panum.503.h
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = farmers
				percent = 0.005
			}
		}
	}

}

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.504.t

	desc = panum.504.d

	flavor = panum.504.f

			panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
			has_building = building_government_administration
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = panum_administrative_evacuation_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
				has_building = building_government_administration
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = panum_administrative_evacuation_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_administrative_evacuation_modifier
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = 0.01
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#The local administration must not collapse.
		name = panum.504.h
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = bureaucrats
				percent = 0.005
			}
		}
	}

		}
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = panum_physician_experienced
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = meticulous
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

#Panum 540: Yellow Fever Treatment
panum.540 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.540.t

	desc = panum.540.d

	flavor = panum.540.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Yellow Fever is losing its horror.
		name = panum.540.g
		panum_add_yellow_fever_treatment_effect = yes
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 4 }
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:panum_physician_var ?= {
					has_trait = panum_yellow_fever
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				remove_trait = panum_yellow_fever
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 541: Into the Feverish Heart
panum.541 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.541.t

	desc = panum.541.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				scope:panum_disease_state = {
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_americas
				}
			}
			desc = panum.541.f_america
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				scope:panum_disease_state = {
					is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_africa
				}
			}
			desc = panum.541.f_africa
		}
	}
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_yellow_fever_investigation.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 2 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

	trigger = {
		var:panum_yellow_fever_treatment_clues_var = 0
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_yellow_fever_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.541.g
		trigger = {
			scope:panum_disease_state = {
				is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_americas
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			panum_add_dubious_yellow_fever_treatment_clues_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.541.h
		trigger = {
			scope:panum_disease_state = {
				is_in_geographic_region = geographic_region_africa
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			panum_add_dubious_yellow_fever_treatment_clues_effect = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

		name = panum.548.g
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = panum_yellow_fever_fork_note_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			panum_add_dubious_yellow_fever_treatment_clues_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#An ounce of prevention is worth a pound of cure.
		name = panum.548.g
		default_option = yes
		highlighted_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = panum_yellow_fever_fork_note_tt
		trigger = {
			theiler_has_yellow_fever_vaccine_trigger = no
			panum_has_miasma_theory_trigger = no
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = theiler_biologist
					has_trait = theiler_microbiologist
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_variable = panum_physician_yellow_fever_fail_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = panum_yellow_fever_vaccine_path_var
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_panum_yellow_fever_vaccine
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}
