	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.570.h
		default_option = yes
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_technology_researched = panum_antitoxins_tech
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						var:panum_physician_experience_var > 200
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.572
					days = { 14 28 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.571
					days = { 14 28 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 574: Vaccine against Yellow Fever
panum.574 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.574.t

	desc = panum.574.d

	flavor = panum.574.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_vaccination.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 200 #Should not happen again
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.574.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_physician_invented_yellow_fever_vaccine_modifier
			years = 25
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = theiler_add_yellow_fever_vaccine_effect_tt
			set_variable = theiler_yellow_fever_vaccine_var
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_variable = theiler_yellow_fever_vaccine_invented_global_var
					}
				}
				set_global_variable = {
					name = theiler_yellow_fever_vaccine_year_global_var
					value = year
				}
				country_definition = {
					set_global_variable = {
						name = theiler_yellow_fever_vaccine_invented_global_var
						value = this
					}
				}
				var:theiler_biologist_var = {
					set_variable = {
						name = theiler_yellow_fever_vaccine_achievement_var
						value = flag:theiler_yellow_fever_vaccine_achievement_loc
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_medical_avant_garde_modifier
					years = 5
				}
				physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 60 }
				panum_medium_add_technology = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_player = yes
						}
						post_notification = theiler_vaccine_yellow_fever_notification
					}
				}
				#For each First Vaccine, add 8 to the medical score
				panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 8 }
			}
			else = {
				physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }
				panum_small_add_technology = yes
				#For each Vaccine, add 4 to the medical score
				panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_measles.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_measles_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Measles!
		name = panum.600.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_measles
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_measles_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_measles_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

		months = 6
	}

		any_scope_state = {

		}
	}

		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_measles_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Is there no cure for this terrible illness?
		name = panum.603.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				percent = 0.002
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 604: Measles paralyzes sailors
panum.604 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.604.t

	desc = panum.604.d

	flavor = panum.604.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_measles.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 3
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_measles_treatment_trigger = no
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_measles_trigger = yes
			OR = {
				has_building = building_fishing_wharf
				has_building = building_whaling_station
			}
			NOT = {
				any_scope_building = {
					OR = {
						is_building_group = bg_fishing
						is_building_group = bg_whaling
					}
					has_modifier = panum_sailor_quarantine_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_measles_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					has_building = building_fishing_wharf
					has_building = building_whaling_station
				}
				NOT = {
					any_scope_building = {
						has_modifier = panum_sailor_quarantine_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#But who then goes to sea?
		name = panum.604.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			every_scope_building = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_building_group = bg_fishing
						is_building_group = bg_whaling
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_sailor_quarantine_modifier
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

#Panum 605: Child Clinic for Measles
panum.605 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.605.t

	desc = panum.605.d

	flavor = panum.605.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_measles.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 12
	}

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_measles_trigger = yes
			has_building = building_government_administration
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_government_administration
				level >= 2
				has_active_production_method = pm_panum_no_clinic
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_measles_trigger = yes
				has_building = building_government_administration
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_government_administration
					level >= 2
					has_active_production_method = pm_panum_no_clinic
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = yes
	        }
			save_scope_as = panum_government_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = panum_government_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#An initiative worth supporting.
		name = panum.605.g
		default_option = yes
		add_treasury = -50000
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_government_administration
				production_method = pm_panum_clinic
			}
		}
		scope:panum_government_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = manzoni_political_tailwind_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#This party only wants to exploit the disease for political purposes.
		name = panum.605.h
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_no_epidemic_corruption_modifier
			years = 3
		}
	}

}

			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

		panum_add_measles_treatment_effect = yes
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 700: Scarlet Fever epidemic
panum.700 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.700.t

	desc = panum.700.d

	flavor = panum.700.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_scarlet.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_scarlet_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Scarlet Fever!
		name = panum.700.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_scarlet
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_scarlet_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_scarlet_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

		}
		modifier = {

				has_trait = panum_physician_experienced
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				has_trait = meticulous
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.740.t

	desc = panum.740.d

	flavor = panum.740.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Scarlet Fever is losing its horror.
		name = panum.740.g
		panum_add_scarlet_treatment_effect = yes
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

######PLAGUE ######

#Panum 800: Plague epidemic (start)
panum.800 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.800.t

	desc = panum.800.d

	flavor = panum.800.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_plague.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_third_plague_global_var
		}
		game_date >= 1894.1.1 #Third Wave started way earlier, but we begin with the Hong Kong outbreak to give enough time to develop antitoxins
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_YUNNAN
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_third_plague_global_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_YUNNAN
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_panum_plague
		}
	}

	option = {	#Plague!
		name = panum.800.g
		default_option = yes
		s:STATE_YUNNAN = {
			start_harvest_condition = panum_plague_condition
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_player = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_player = yes
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = panum.804
						days = { 20 30 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 803: Plague epidemic
panum.803 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.800.t

	desc = panum.803.d

	flavor = panum.800.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_plague.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_plague_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Plague!
		name = panum.803.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_plague
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_plague_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_plague_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

			}

		}

		}

		name = panum.805.h

			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				percent = 0.005
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				pop_type = aristocrats
				percent = 0.003
			}
		}
	}

			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Burn clothes, furniture and even houses if necessary!
		name = panum.811.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_plague_burn_everything_modifier
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata =upper
				value = 0.05
			}
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				strata = middle
				value = 0.03
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#That is not necessary.
		name = panum.811.h
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			kill_population_percent_in_state = {
				percent = 0.002
			}
		}
	}
}

				value = 0.02
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#This is too costly

	}

	flavor = panum.840.f

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Scarlet Fever is losing its horror.
		name = panum.840.g
		panum_add_plague_treatment_effect = yes
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

		}
		has_variable = panum_plague_tissue_sample_var
		var:panum_plague_treatment_clues_var >= 5
	}

			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope

		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_plague_trigger = yes
			}

		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_plague_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
		panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 8 }
		theiler_add_plague_pathogen_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time

		base = 1

#Panum 900: Diphteria epidemic
panum.900 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.900.t

	desc = panum.900.d

	flavor = panum.900.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_diphteria.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_diphteria_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Diphteria
		name = panum.900.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_diphteria
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_diphteria_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_diphteria_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Panum 940: Diphteria Treatment
panum.940 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.940.t

	desc = panum.940.d

	flavor = panum.940.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Diphteria is losing its horror.
		name = panum.940.g
		panum_add_diphteria_treatment_effect = yes
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						has_variable = panum_the_shadow_var
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.963
					days = { 300 500 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 952: Treating Diphteria
panum.952 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.952.t

	desc = panum.952.d

	flavor = panum.952.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_2char

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope
	right_icon = scope:panum_son_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 100
	}

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		create_character = {
			first_name = mr_null
			last_name = mr_null
			female = no
			age = 6
			save_scope_as = panum_son_scope
		}
		scope:panum_son_scope = {
			place_character_in_void = 120
		}
	}

	option = {	#Treat the boy with iron perchlorate.
		name = panum.952.g
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				9 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = panum.953
						days = { 3 7 }
					}
				}
				1 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = panum.954
						days = { 3 7 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Treat the boy with iron perchlorate.
		name = panum.952.h
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						has_trait = panum_surgeon
						var:panum_physician_experience_var > 200
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.954
					days = { 3 7 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.953
					days = { 3 7 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Examine a tissue sample with the microscope.
		name = panum.952.i
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = theiler_biologist
					has_trait = cruel
					has_trait = ruthless
					has_trait = reckless
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = panum.955
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:panum_son_scope = {
				free_character_from_void = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1000: Polio epidemic
panum.1000 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1000.t

	desc = panum.1000.d

	flavor = panum.1000.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_polio.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		panum_set_polio_state_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Polio
		name = panum.1000.g
		default_option = yes
		show_as_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				}
				add_journal_entry = {
					type = je_panum_polio
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_polio_treatment_trigger = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_polio_treatment_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop pestering me!
		name = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = panum_stop_epidemic_notification_events_tt
			set_variable = panum_no_disease_popup_events_var
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1001: Polio epidemic - Start
panum.1001 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1001.t

	desc = panum.1001.d

	flavor = panum.1000.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_polio.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		#Moved the Trigger into the effect of an on_action
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				average_sol <= 35
				total_urbanization >= 1000
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_panum_polio
		}
	}

	option = {	#Polio is now an epidemic disease.
		name = panum.1001.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			state_region = {
				start_harvest_condition = panum_polio_condition
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_player = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_player = yes
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = panum.1002
						days = { 20 30 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

			}

			limit = {

				NOT = {

				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_polio_generation_modifier

			}

#Panum 1006: Politician establishes Polio Foundation
panum.1006 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1006.t

	desc = panum.1006.d

	flavor = panum.1006.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_polio.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 12
	}

	trigger = {
		has_variable = panum_polio_survivors_var
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_polio_foundation_var
		}
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = panum_polio_foundation_modifier
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_polio_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_polio_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
    			is_in_government = no
	        }
			save_scope_as = panum_opposition_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = panum_opposition_leader
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#A true philanthropist
		name = panum.1006.g
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = panum_polio_foundation_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_polio_foundation_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		scope:panum_opposition_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = manzoni_political_tailwind_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#And the upcoming election is pure coincidence, I assume?
		name = panum.1006.h
		scope:panum_opposition_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_mocked_polio_foundation_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1007: Polio Clinic
panum.1007 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1007.t
	desc = panum.1007.d
	flavor = panum.1007.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_polio.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		months = 12
	}

	trigger = {
		religion = {
			has_discrimination_trait = heritage_christian
		}
		OR = {
			has_law = law_type:law_state_religion
			has_law = law_type:law_freedom_of_conscience
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_polio_trigger = yes
			has_building = building_government_administration
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_government_administration
				level >= 2
				has_active_production_method = pm_panum_no_clinic
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_polio_trigger = yes
				has_building = building_government_administration
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_government_administration
					level >= 2
					has_active_production_method = pm_panum_no_clinic
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		create_character = {
			female = yes
			interest_group = ig_devout
			save_scope_as = panum_polio_nurse
		}
		scope:panum_polio_nurse = {
			place_character_in_void = 120
		}
	}

	option = {	#Thank you, Sister Polio Nurse.
		name = panum.1006.g
		default_option = yes

		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			activate_production_method = {
				building_type = building_government_administration
				production_method = pm_panum_clinic
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:panum_polio_nurse = {
				free_character_from_void = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1040: Polio Treatment
panum.1040 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1040.t

	desc = panum.1040.d

	flavor = panum.1040.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		#Sets up a variable that sets the treatment title
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			value = { 1 10 }
		}
		round_variable = {
			name = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			nearest = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Polio is losing its horror.
		name = panum.1040.g
		panum_add_polio_treatment_effect = yes
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_title_randomizer_var
			remove_variable = panum_disease_title_var
		}
	}
}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

		years = 5 #Should not happen again in this epidemic
	}

		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_polio_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#This is unacceptable!
		name = panum.1055.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_polio_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:panum_physician_var = {
					has_trait = cruel
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				remove_trait = cruel
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			add_trait = charismatic
		}
	}

	option = {	#This could be the start of a second career.
		name = panum.1055.h
		panum_add_x_polio_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:panum_physician_var = {
					has_trait = cruel
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				remove_trait = cruel
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			add_trait = panum_psychiatrist
		}
	}

	option = {	#Let these records disappear quickly.
		name = panum.1055.i
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1062: Iron Lung
panum.1062 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.261.t

	desc = panum.261.d

	flavor = panum.261.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_2char

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope
	right_icon = scope:gaudi_engineer_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_iron_lung_var
		}
		tesla_has_engineer = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = panum_iron_lung_global_var
				}
			}
			country_definition = {
				set_global_variable = {
					name = panum_iron_lung_global_var
					value = this
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = {
				name = panum_iron_lung_year_global_var
				value = year
			}
		}
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		set_variable = panum_iron_lung_var
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		var:tesla_engineer_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_polio_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#It's about saving human lives.
		name = panum.1062.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_polio_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 4 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = panum_iron_lung_global_var
				}
			}
			var:tesla_engineer_var = {
				set_variable = {
					name = panum_physician_achievement_iron_lung_inventor_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_iron_lung_inventor_loc
				}
			}
			panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_iron_lung_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

			has_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
		has_technology_researched = panum_vitamins_tech
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_polio_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Precisely observed.
		name = panum.1064.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_add_x_polio_treatment_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_treatment_search_ongoing_var #We try to have only one event at a time
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1100: Spanish Flu
panum.1100 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1100.t

	desc = panum.1100.d

	flavor = panum.1100.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_journal_entry = je_panum_spanish_flu
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		panum_set_spanish_flu_state_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_country_type = decentralized }
			}
			add_journal_entry = {
				type = je_panum_spanish_flu
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Spanish Flu
		name = panum.1100.g
		default_option = yes
	}
}

#Panum 1101: Spanish Flu - Historical Start
panum.1101 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1101.t

	desc = panum.1101.d

	flavor = panum.1101.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = panum_historical_spanish_flu_rule
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_spanish_flu_pandemic_global_var
		}
		game_date >= 1918.1.1 #Patient Zero; however, Spanish Flu started way earlier
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_NEW_CASTILE #Spanish Flu did not start in Spain, but we get the name from here
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_spanish_flu_pandemic_global_var
		country_definition = {
			set_global_variable = {
				name = panum_spanish_flu_originator_country
				value = this
			}
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_NEW_CASTILE
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
			set_variable = panum_spanish_flu_originator_state
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_panum_spanish_flu
		}
	}

	option = {	#Spanish Flu Pandemic started
		name = panum.1101.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			state_region = {
				start_harvest_condition = panum_spanish_flu_condition
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1102: Spanish Flu - Dynamic Start
panum.1102 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	type = country_event

	title = panum.1102.t

	desc = panum.1102.d

	flavor = panum.1102.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = panum_dynamic_spanish_flu_rule
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_spanish_flu_pandemic_global_var
		}
		game_date >= 1905.1.1
		game_date < 1920.1.1
		country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			OR = {
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_railway
					production_method = pm_electric_trains
				}
				is_production_method_active = {
					building_type = building_railway
					production_method = pm_diesel_trains
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_spanish_flu_pandemic_global_var
		country_definition = {
			set_global_variable = {
				name = panum_spanish_flu_originator_country
				value = this
			}
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
				OR = {
					is_production_method_active = {
						building_type = building_railway
						production_method = pm_electric_trains
					}
					is_production_method_active = {
						building_type = building_railway
						production_method = pm_diesel_trains
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
			set_variable = panum_spanish_flu_originator_state
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_panum_spanish_flu
		}
	}

	option = {	#Spanish Flu Pandemic started
		name = panum.1101.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			state_region = {
				start_harvest_condition = panum_spanish_flu_condition
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1103: Pandemic Policy
panum.1103 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT

	title = panum.1103.t
	desc = plague.5.d
	flavor = plague.5.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	duration = 3

	immediate = {
	}

	option = { # lockdown!
		name = plague.5.a
		custom_tooltip = panum.1103.a.tt
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
				}
				remove_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
			}			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = panum_spanish_flu_measures_var
				}
				remove_variable = panum_spanish_flu_measures_var
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # social distancing and masks
		name = plague.5.b
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = panum.1103.b.tt
		set_variable = {
			name = panum_spanish_flu_measures_var
		}
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
				}
				remove_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
			}			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
				}
				remove_variable = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # think about the economy!
		name = plague.5.c
		custom_tooltip = panum.1103.c.tt
		remove_variable = panum_spanish_flu_measures_var
		remove_variable = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
				}
				remove_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
			}
			else = {
				remove_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_pandemic_policy_event_active_var
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1104: Pandemic fading
panum.1104 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:panum_flu_fading_state

	title = panum.1104.t
	desc = panum.1104.d
	flavor = panum.1104.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_fading_modifier
			}
			panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
			OR = {
				has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
				has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_fading_modifier
				}
				panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_flu_fading_state
		}
	}

	option = { # lockdown!
		name = panum.1104.g
		scope:panum_flu_fading_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_spanish_flu_fading_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			has_variable = panum_physician_var
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				has_trait = panum_physician_famous
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_health_system
				value >= 4
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_modifier = panum_medical_techniques_level_6_modifier
				has_modifier = panum_medical_techniques_level_7_modifier
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1105: Pandemic disappearing

	type = country_event
	placement = scope:panum_flu_disappearing_state

	title = panum.1105.t

	flavor = panum.1105.f

			panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
			has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_fading_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_recent_pandemic_policy_change_modifier
			days = 180
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_flu_disappearing_state
		}
	}

		scope:panum_flu_disappearing_state = {
			remove_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_fading_modifier
			set_variable = panum_recent_spanish_flu_var
			state_region = {
				finish_harvest_condition = panum_spanish_flu_condition
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			has_variable = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			has_variable = panum_physician_var
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				has_trait = panum_physician_famous
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_health_system
				value >= 4
			}
			add = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_modifier = panum_medical_techniques_level_6_modifier
				has_modifier = panum_medical_techniques_level_7_modifier
			}
			add = 1
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1107: Pandemic impacts war support
panum.1107 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	title = panum.1107.t
	desc = panum.1107.d
	flavor = panum.1107.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		is_at_war = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
		}
		any_interest_group = {
			is_in_government = no
			NOT = { has_modifier = plague_war }
			leader = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_pacifist
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
				panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				is_in_government = no
				NOT = { has_modifier = plague_war }
				leader = {
					has_ideology = ideology:ideology_pacifist
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = pacifist_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = pacifist_leader
			}
		}
	}

	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = panum_spanish_flu_pandemic_over_global_var
	}

	option = { # gain turmoil
		name = panum.1107.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
			}
		}
		scope:pacifist_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = plague_war
				months = 24
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # propaganda and reassurance
		name = panum.1107.h
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = mass_propaganda
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_health_system
				value >= 3
			}
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = small_radicals
			}
		}
		scope:pacifist_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = plague_war
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # censorship
		name = panum.1107.i
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_law = law_type:law_censorship
				has_law = law_type:law_outlawed_dissent
			}
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = small_radicals
			}
		}
		scope:pacifist_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = plague_war
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 1108: Poverty and evictions
panum.1108 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:panum_disease_state

	title = panum.1108.t
	desc = panum.1108.d
	flavor = panum.1108.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
			OR = {
				has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
				has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
			}
			state_unemployment_rate >= 0.2
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
				panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
				}
				state_unemployment_rate >= 0.2
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_disease_state
		}
		ig:ig_landowners = {
			save_scope_as = landowner_ig
		}
	}

	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = panum_spanish_flu_pandemic_over_global_var
	}

	option = { # rent freeze and eviction ban
		name = panum.1108.g
		scope:landowner_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = plague_eviction_ban
				months = 12
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_interest_group = {
					leader = {
						has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anarchist
					}
				}
			}
			every_interest_group = {
				limit = {
					has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anarchist
				}
				add_modifier = plague_eviction_ban_anarchist
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Rely on social security
		name = panum.1108.h
		trigger = {
			institution_investment_level = {
				institution = institution_social_security
				value = 3
			}
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = plague_welfare_cost
			months = 12
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_interest_group = {
					leader = {
						OR = {
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_vanguardist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_social_democrat
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_interest_group = {
				limit = {
					leader = {
						OR = {
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_vanguardist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_social_democrat
						}
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = plague_welfare_reliance
					months = 12
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # We don't care about poor people
		name = panum.1108.i
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_disease_state = {
			add_radicals_in_state = {
				value = medium_radicals
				strata = lower
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_interest_group = {
					leader = {
						OR = {
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_vanguardist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_social_democrat
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anarchist
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_interest_group = {
				limit = {
					leader = {
						OR = {
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_vanguardist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_communist
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_social_democrat
							has_ideology = ideology:ideology_anarchist
						}
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = plague_no_poverty_measures
					months = 12
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_spanish_flu.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_variable = panum_spanish_flu_measures_var
			has_variable = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			panum_state_has_spanish_flu_trigger = yes
			OR = {
				has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
				has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
		}
		any_interest_group = {
			has_ideology = ideology:ideology_laissez_faire
			is_in_government = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				has_ideology = ideology:ideology_laissez_faire
				is_in_government = no
			}
			save_scope_as = anti_mask_ig
			leader = {
				save_scope_as = anti_mask_ig_leader
			}
		}
	}

	cancellation_trigger = {
		has_global_variable = panum_spanish_flu_pandemic_over_global_var
	}
	
	option = { # Ignore their demands
		name = panum.1109.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:anti_mask_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = anti_mask_ignored
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Cave in to demands
		name = panum.1109.h
		remove_variable = panum_spanish_flu_measures_var
		remove_variable = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_var
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
					has_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
				}
			}
			remove_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_lockdown_modifier
			remove_modifier = panum_spanish_flu_measures_modifier
		}
		scope:anti_mask_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = anti_mask_appeased
				months = 12
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_recent_pandemic_policy_change_modifier
			days = 180
		}
	}
	option = { # Discredit their movement with science
		name = panum.1109.i
		trigger = {
			panum_has_physician = yes
			panum_has_miasma_theory_trigger = no
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				OR = {
					has_trait = panum_physician_experienced
					has_trait = panum_physician_famous
				}
			}
		}
		highlighted_option = yes
		scope:anti_mask_ig = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = anti_mask_discredited
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		}
		triggered_desc = {

		}

#Panum 2001: Medical Congress - Invitation
panum.2001 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2001.t
	desc = panum.2001.d
	flavor = panum.2001.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_medical_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	immediate = {
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2001.g # Invite the leading medical nations
		if = {
			limit = {
				panum_has_physician = yes
			}
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				set_variable = {
					name = panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_loc
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				theiler_has_microbiologist_trigger = yes
			}
			var:theiler_biologist_var ?= {
				set_variable = {
					name = panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_loc
				}
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_congress_attend_modifier
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					this = ROOT 
				}
				OR = {
					panum_has_physician = yes
					theiler_has_microbiologist_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = panum.2002
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_physician = yes
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2003
					days = { 20 40 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					theiler_has_microbiologist_trigger = yes
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2004
					days = { 20 40 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2005
					days = { 20 40 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_congress_host_country
		}
	}

			limit = {
				panum_has_physician = yes

					name = panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_loc
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				theiler_has_microbiologist_trigger = yes
			}
			var:theiler_biologist_var ?= {
				set_variable = {
					name = panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_attended_medical_congress_loc
				}
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_congress_attend_modifier
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_physician = yes
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2003
					days = { 20 40 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					theiler_has_microbiologist_trigger = yes
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2004
					days = { 20 40 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2005
					days = { 20 40 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 2003: Medical Congress - Description & Treatment for Physician
panum.2003 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2003.t
	desc = panum.2003.d
	flavor = panum.2003.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_medical_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_congress_host_country
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2003.h #Cholera
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					panum_has_cholera_description_trigger = no
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = panum_congress_attend_modifier
						NOT = {
							this = ROOT
						}
						panum_has_cholera_description_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				AND = {
					panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = no
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = panum_congress_attend_modifier
						NOT = {
							this = ROOT
						}
						panum_has_cholera_treatment_trigger = yes
					}
				}

#Panum 2004: Medical Congress - Pathogen & Vaccine for Biologist
panum.2004 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2004.t
	desc = panum.2004.d
	flavor = panum.2004.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_medical_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_congress_host_country
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2003.h #Cholera
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					theiler_has_cholera_pathogen_trigger = no
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = panum_congress_attend_modifier
						NOT = {
							this = ROOT
						}
						theiler_has_cholera_pathogen_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				AND = {
					theiler_has_cholera_vaccine_trigger = no
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = panum_congress_attend_modifier
						NOT = {
							this = ROOT
						}
						theiler_has_cholera_vaccine_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				theiler_has_cholera_pathogen_trigger = no
				any_country = {
					has_modifier = panum_congress_attend_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
					theiler_has_cholera_pathogen_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = theiler_add_cholera_pathogen_effect_tt
				set_variable = theiler_cholera_pathogen_var
			}

			}

				theiler_has_smallpox_pathogen_trigger = no

					has_modifier = panum_congress_attend_modifier

						this = ROOT
					}
					theiler_has_smallpox_pathogen_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = theiler_add_smallpox_pathogen_effect_tt
				set_variable = theiler_smallpox_pathogen_var
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				theiler_has_smallpox_vaccine_trigger = no
				any_country = {
					has_modifier = panum_congress_attend_modifier
					NOT = {
						this = ROOT
					}
					theiler_has_smallpox_vaccine_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = theiler_add_smallpox_vaccine_effect_tt

			}

#Panum 2005: Medical Congress - Topic
panum.2005 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2005.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				any_country = {
					has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
					has_variable = panum_medical_congress_general_var
				}
			}
			desc = panum.2005.d_general
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					any_country = {
						has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
						has_variable = panum_medical_congress_general_var
					}
				}
			}
			desc = panum.2005.d_special
		}
	}
	flavor = panum.2005.f

	duration = 3

	event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_medical_congress.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_congress_host_country
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2005.g #The event was worth it.
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		biologist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		panum_add_medical_congress_clues_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_has_miasma_theory_trigger = yes
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2006
					days = { 14 28 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					panum_can_get_medical_innovation_trigger = yes
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2007
					days = { 14 28 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2009
					days = { 60 90 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_congress_host_country
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2006.g #This evidence cannot be dismissed out of hand.
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = panum_congress_host_modifier
			}
			panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
		}
		else = {
			panum_add_x_germ_theory_clues_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					panum_can_get_medical_innovation_trigger = yes
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2007
					days = { 14 28 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.2009
					days = { 60 90 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Panum 2100: Physician Recruitment
panum.2100 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2100.t

	desc = panum.2100.d

	flavor = panum.2100.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_new_physician_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_academy.dds"

	duration = 1

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		create_new_character_base_effect = { CHARACTER = physician PROJECT = panum }
	}

	option = {
		name = panum.2100.g #Epidemiology
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = panum_vaccination_tech
			NOT = {
				scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
					has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
				}
			}
		}
		scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_epidemiologist
		}
		panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = panum.2100.h #Surgery
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
					has_trait = panum_surgeon
				}
			}
		}
		scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_surgeon
		}
		panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = panum.2100.i #Psychiatry
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = psychiatry
			NOT = {
				scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
					has_trait = panum_psychiatrist
				}
			}
		}
		scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_psychiatrist
		}
		panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = panum.2100.j #Military Medicine
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = triage
			NOT = {
				scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
					has_trait = panum_military_physician
				}
			}
		}
		scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_military_physician
		}
		panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_variable = panum_physician_recruitment_var
		}
	}
}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_first_clinic_opened_var
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			has_building = building_government_administration
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_government_administration
				level >= 5
				has_active_production_method = pm_panum_clinic
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_first_clinic_opened_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_government_administration
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_government_administration
					level >= 5
					has_active_production_method = pm_panum_clinic
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_clinic_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Surgery
		name = panum.2102.g
		trigger = {
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = panum_surgeon
				}
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			add_trait = panum_surgeon
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
	}

	option = {	#Psychiatry
		name = panum.2102.h
		trigger = {
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = panum_psychiatrist
				}
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			add_trait = panum_psychiatrist
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
	}

	option = {	#Epidemiology
		name = panum.2102.i
		trigger = {
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = panum_epidemiologist
				}
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			add_trait = panum_epidemiologist
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
	}

	option = {	#Military Medicine
		name = panum.2102.j
		trigger = {
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				NOT = {
					has_trait = panum_military_physician
				}
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			add_trait = panum_military_physician
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
	}

	option = {	#Experience
		name = panum.2102.k
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
		}
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
	}
}

	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2123.t

	desc = panum.2123.d

	flavor = panum.2123.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_2char

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope
	right_icon = scope:panum_victim_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	cooldown = {
		years = 100
	}

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = panum_anthropological_criminology_modifier
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			has_variable = panum_lombroso_var
		}
		has_variable = panum_biological_determinism_var
		any_scope_character = {
			is_ruler = no
			is_busy = no
			NOT = {
				has_variable = panum_not_a_criminal_var
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_variable = panum_not_a_criminal_var
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_victim_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#This person actually has a criminal face.
		name = panum.2123.g
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = panum_crime_face_var
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		scope:panum_victim_scope = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#The doctor goes too far with his accusations!
		name = panum.2123.h
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = -5 }
		scope:panum_victim_scope = {
			set_variable = panum_not_a_criminal_var
		}
	}
}

				}

		}

		name = panum.2124.g
		lepsius_set_new_anthropologist_as_anthropologist_effect = yes
	}

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			has_trait = cruel
		}
		panum_has_active_physician_no_tooltip_trigger = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
	}

		name = panum.2205.g
		default_option = yes
		panum_small_add_technology = yes

					var:panum_physician_var = {

					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				5 = {}
				1 = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						add_trait = psychological_affliction
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#The students should learn how to dissect animals.
		name = panum.2205.h
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						has_trait = psychological_affliction
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = {}
				1 = {
					var:panum_physician_var = {
						add_trait = psychological_affliction
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#This is clearly going too far.
		name = panum.2205.i
	}

}

			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
	}

		name = panum.2221.g
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_variable = panum_anthrax_disease_global_var
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = panum_anthrax_disease_global_var
				var:panum_physician_var = {
					set_variable = {
						name = panum_physician_achievement_anthrax_disease_var
						value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_anthrax_disease_loc
					}
				}
			panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 1 }
			panum_small_add_technology = yes
		}
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_woolsorters_disease_modifier
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			panum_disease_investigation_remove_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

### Medical Innovations ###

#Panum 2411: Aspirin
panum.2411 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	placement = scope:panum_aspirin_state_scope

	title = panum.2411.t
	desc = panum.2411.d
	flavor = panum.2411.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_2char

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope
	right_icon = scope:mendelejew_chemist_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_aspirin_global_var
		}
		mendelejew_has_chemist = yes
		has_technology_researched = theiler_microbiology_tech
		any_scope_building = {
			is_building_type = building_chemical_plant
			level >= 3
		}
		var:dubois_specimen >= 5000
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = {
			name = panum_aspirin_year_global_var
			value = year
		}
		country_definition = {
			set_global_variable = {
				name = panum_aspirin_global_var
				value = this
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		var:mendelejew_chemist_var = {
			save_scope_as = mendelejew_chemist_scope
		}
		random_scope_building = {
			limit = {
				is_building_type = building_chemical_plant
				level >= 3
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_aspirin_building_scope
			state = {
				save_scope_as = panum_aspirin_state_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2411.g #The drug will be the starting point for further medical research.
		panum_small_add_technology = yes
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 20 }
		var:mendelejew_chemist_var = {
			set_variable = {
				name = mendelejew_chemist_achievement_aspirin_inventor_var
				value = flag:mendelejew_chemist_achievement_aspirin_inventor_loc
			}
		}
		panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = -5000 }
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2411.h #Chemistry is sure to open up even more spectacular discoveries.
		mendelejew_small_add_technology = yes
		chemist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 20 }
		var:mendelejew_chemist_var = {
			set_variable = {
				name = mendelejew_chemist_achievement_aspirin_inventor_var
				value = flag:mendelejew_chemist_achievement_aspirin_inventor_loc
			}
		}
		panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = -5000 }
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2411.i #The pharmaceutical industry will benefit from this.
		default_option = yes
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		chemist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		scope:panum_aspirin_building_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_aspirin_factory_modifier
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_variable = {
				name = mendelejew_chemist_achievement_aspirin_inventor_var
				value = flag:mendelejew_chemist_achievement_aspirin_inventor_loc
			}
		}
		panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 2 }
		dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = -5000 }
	}
}

#Panum 2412: X-Rays

			has_global_variable = panum_xray_global_var
		}
		curie_has_physicist = yes
		has_technology_researched = verrier_modern_physics_tech
		any_scope_state = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_government_administration
				has_active_production_method = pm_panum_hospital
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_xray_var
		set_global_variable = {
			name = panum_xray_year_global_var
			value = year
		}
		country_definition = {
			set_global_variable = {
				name = panum_xray_global_var
				value = this
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		var:curie_physicist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curie_physicist_scope
		}
		random_scope_building = {
			limit = {
				is_building_type = building_government_administration
				has_active_production_method = pm_panum_hospital
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_xray_building_scope
			state = {
				save_scope_as = panum_xray_state_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2412.g #Spooky - like seeing your own death.
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		physicist_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_xray_modifier
		}
		var:curie_physicist_var = {
			set_variable = panum_physician_achievement_xray_inventor_var
		}
		panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 4 }
	}
}

		set_variable = panum_cardiopulmonary_bypass_var
		set_global_variable = {
			name = panum_cardiopulmonary_bypass_year_global_var
			value = year
		}
		country_definition = {
			set_global_variable = {
				name = panum_cardiopulmonary_bypass_global_var
				value = this
			}
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = panum.2417.g #And people thought Frankenstein was a horror novel!
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 30 }
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = { AMOUNT = 60 }
		panum_medium_add_technology = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_cardiopulmonary_bypass_modifier
		}
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			set_variable = {
				name = panum_physician_achievement_cardiopulmonary_bypass_inventor_var
				value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_cardiopulmonary_bypass_inventor_loc
			}
		}
		panum_add_x_medical_score_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 3 }
	}
}

#Panum 2500: Advanced Medical Support
panum.2500 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2500.t
	desc = panum.2500.d
	flavor = panum.2500.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:panum_physician_var = {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = panum_physician_advanced_medical_support_var } }
			set_variable = {
				name = panum_physician_advanced_medical_support_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = panum_physician_advanced_medical_support_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = panum_physician_var }
			var:panum_physician_var = {
				set_variable = {
					name = panum_physician_achievement_military_medicine_project_finished_var
					value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_military_medicine_project_finished_loc
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = panum.2500.g #A wonder of technology!
		default_option = yes

		custom_tooltip = panum_advanced_medical_support_mobilization_option_tt
		panum_medium_add_technology = yes
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
	}
}

	desc = panum.2600.d
	flavor = panum.2600.f

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_psychiatry.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_psychiatry.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_variable = panum_asylum_inauguration_happened
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			set_variable = {
				name = panum_physician_achievement_inaugurated_asylum_var
				value = flag:panum_physician_achievement_inaugurated_asylum_loc
			}
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_panum_asylum
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_asylum_state
		}
	}

		name = panum.2600.g #Finally the right place for politicians, journalists, actors...
		default_option = yes
		dubois_add_x_academy_progress = {
			AMOUNT = 30
		}
	}
}

#Panum 2622: The Strange Cause of Phineas Gage
panum.2622 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	placement = scope:panum_phineas_gage_state

	title = panum.2622.t
	desc = panum.2622.d
	flavor = panum.2622.f

	gui_window = event_window_2char

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope
	right_icon = scope:panum_phineas_gage

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_psychiatry.dds"

	trigger = {
		panum_has_active_physician_no_tooltip_trigger = yes
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_phineas_gage_global_var
		}
		NOT = {
			has_technology_researched = psychoanalysis
		}
		has_technology_researched = psychiatry
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			has_trait = panum_psychiatrist
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_railway
				level = 0
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_phineas_gage_global_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_railway
					level = 0
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_phineas_gage_state
		}
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
		create_character = {
			female = no
			save_scope_as = panum_phineas_gage
		}
		scope:panum_phineas_gage = {
			place_character_in_void = 120
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = panum.2622.g #So the psyche and brain areas are connected?
		default_option = yes
		panum_small_add_technology = yes
		panum_add_x_psycho_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 50 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:panum_phineas_gage = {
				free_character_from_void = no
			}
		}
	}
}

		panum_small_add_technology = yes
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 15 }
		panum_add_x_psycho_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 50 }
	}
}

#Panum 2626: The Dr. [ROOT.Var('panum_physician_var').GetCharacter.GetFullName] Show
panum.2626 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.2626.t
	desc = panum.2626.d
	flavor = panum.2626.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:panum_physician_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_psychiatry.dds"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = panum_dr_frasier_crane_var
		}
		has_technology_researched = radio
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			OR = {
				has_trait = panum_psychiatrist
				has_trait = panum_psychologist
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = panum_dr_frasier_crane_var
		var:panum_physician_var ?= {
			save_scope_as = panum_physician_scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = panum.2626.g #This is Dr. Frasier Crane.
		default_option = yes
		physician_experience_gain_effect = { AMOUNT = 10 }
		panum_add_x_psycho_points_effect = { AMOUNT = 25 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:panum_physician_var ?= {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = panum_psychiatrist
					}
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				add_trait = panum_psychiatrist
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:panum_physician_var ?= {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = panum_psychologist
					}
				}
			}
			var:panum_physician_var ?= {
				add_trait = panum_psychologist
			}
		}
	}
	
}

#Panum 3000: The Red Cross
panum.3000 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	placement = scope:panum_red_cross_state

	type = country_event

	title = panum.3000.t

	desc = panum.3000.d

	flavor = panum.3000.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_red_cross.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_red_cross_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#A decisive step forward in international cooperation.
		name = panum.3000.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_red_cross_state = {
			create_building = {
				building = "building_panum_red_cross"
				level = 1
			}
			state_region = {
				set_global_variable = { #This is used in the GUI to display the state
            		name = panum_red_cross_seat_global_var
           			value = this
        		}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_player = no
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_player = yes
					}
					trigger_event = {
						id = panum.3001
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

}
