	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_panum_red_cross
			}
			save_scope_as = panum_red_cross_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#We join this organization as a founding member.
		name = panum.3001.g
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = panum_red_cross_member_var
		add_modifier = {
			name = panum_red_cross_member_modifier
		}
		change_infamy = -3
		trigger = {
			is_country_type = recognized
			infamy < 35
			OR = {
				has_technology_researched = modern_nursing
				has_technology_researched = human_rights
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Interesting.
		name = panum.3001.h
	}

}

		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_red_cross_global_var
		}
		game_date >= 1862.1.1
		game_date < 1870.1.1
		c:SWI ?= this
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_red_cross_global_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_capital = yes
			}

		}

			}

				set_global_variable = { #This is used in the GUI to display the state

           			value = this
        		}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

				}

					limit = {

					}

#Panum 3021: A Red Cross Medic
panum.3021 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event
	
	title = panum.3021.t
	desc = panum.3021.d
	flavor = panum.3021.f
	
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_red_cross_war.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"
	
	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		panum_has_physician = no
		has_variable = panum_red_cross_member_var
		any_scope_war = {
			any_scope_front = {
				any_scope_general = {
					owner = ROOT
					this.commander_military_formation = {
						OR = {
							has_mobilization_option = mobilization_option:mobilization_option_first_aid
							has_mobilization_option = mobilization_option:mobilization_option_field_hospitals
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		ROOT = { save_scope_as = flying_circus_home }
		create_new_character_base_effect = { CHARACTER = physician PROJECT = panum }
		random_scope_war = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_front = {
					any_scope_general = {
						owner = ROOT
						this.commander_military_formation = {
							OR = {
								has_mobilization_option = mobilization_option:mobilization_option_first_aid
								has_mobilization_option = mobilization_option:mobilization_option_field_hospitals
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = flying_circus_war
		}
	}

	option = { #This will be the beginning of a unique career.
		name = panum.3021.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:panum_new_physician_scope = {
			add_trait = panum_red_cross
		}
		panum_set_new_physician_as_physician_effect = yes
	}
}

#Panum 3031: First Convention becomes a binding Convention
panum.3031 = {
	dlc = dlc_morgenrote

	type = country_event

	title = panum.3031.t

	desc = panum.3031.d

	flavor = panum.3031.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/panum_pictures/panum_convention.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_medicine.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		has_global_variable = panum_first_convention_proposed_global_var
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = panum_first_convention_binding_global_var
		}
		panum_first_geneva_convention_becomes_binding_trigger = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_panum_red_cross
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = panum_first_convention_binding_global_var
	}

	option = {	#A globally valid international law is created.
		name = panum.3031.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = panum_first_geneva_convention_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = panum_first_geneva_convention_modifier
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = panum_red_cross_member_var
					NOT = { this = ROOT }
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = panum_first_geneva_convention_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = panum_first_geneva_convention_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_player = yes
					has_variable = panum_red_cross_member_var
					NOT = { this = ROOT }
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = panum.3034
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
